Source Code

This is an attempt to recreate Luminary 99 Rev 2, otherwise known as LUM99R2, from Luminary 99 Rev 1 and ephemeris data from Luminary 116. The differences are confined to the last 10-12 lines of the CONTROLLED CONSTANTS. Luminary 99 Rev 1 source-code was transcribed from a printout in the MIT Museum, while Luminary 116 source code was transcribed from a printout belonging to Don Eyles. AGC developer James Kernan, the "rope mother" for the Apollo 11 Lunar Module's AGC, explains as follows: "At the last minute, Dan Lickly, our chief engineer, appeared with ephemerides updates and it took two tries to get it right. The result was that we created Lum99 Revision 1 and Lum99 Revision 2." It is suspected that the former is what's in the MIT Museum, and the latter is what we are trying to recreate here. As for which revision actually flew in Apollo 11, all of the other available surviving evidence points to Rev 1 rather than to Rev 2, so we're just not sure!

020786,000030:                                                                                                  #  RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM 20
020787,000031: 
020788,000032:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
020789,000033: 
020790,000034:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
020791,000035:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
020792,000036: 
020793,000037:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
020794,000038: 
020795,000039:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO CONTROL THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR FROM
020796,000040:                                                                                                  #        STARTUP THROUGH ACQUISITION AND LOCKON TO THE CSM AND TO UPDATE EITHER 
020797,000041:                                                                                                  #        THE LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (AS SPECIFIED BY THE ASTRONAUT BY DSKY ENTRY)
020798,000042:                                                                                                  #        ON THE BASIS OF THE RR TRACKING DATA.
020799,000043: 
020800,000044:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
020801,000045: 
020802,000046:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E20E
020803,000047: 
020804,000048:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
020805,000049: 
020806,000050:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      FLAGUP
020807,000051:                                                                                                  #        GOFLASH (PINBALL-DISPLAY)                       FLAGDOWN
020808,000052:                                                                                                  #        R23LEM  (MANUAL ACQUISITION)                    BANKCALL
020809,000053:                                                                                                  #        LS201   (LOS DETERMINATION)                     TASKOVER
020810,000054:                                                                                                  #        LS202   (RANGE LIMIT TEST)
020811,000055:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE)
020812,000056:                                                                                                  #        R21LEM  (RR DESIGNATE)                          ENDOFJOB
020813,000057:                                                                                                  #        R22LEM  (DATA READ)                             GOPERF1
020814,000058:                                                                                                  #        R31LEM  (RENDEZVOUS PARAMETER DISPLAY)  
020815,000059:                                                                                                  #        PRIOLARM (PRIORITY DISPLAY)
020816,000060: 
020817,000061:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
020818,000062: 
020819,000063:                                                                                                  #        P20 MAY BE TERMINATED IN TWO WAYS - ASTRONAUT SELECTION OF IDLING
020820,000064:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E
020821,000065: 
020822,000066:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
020823,000067: 
020824,000068:                                                                                                  #        RANGE GREATER THAN 400 NM DISPLAY
020825,000069: 
020826,000070:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
020827,000071: 
020828,000072:                                                                                                  #        TRKMKCNT = NO OF RENDEZVOUS TRACKING MARKS TAKEN (COUNTER)
020829,000073: 
020830,000074:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
020831,000075: 
020832,000076:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
020833,000077: 
020834,000078:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, RNDVZFLG, ACMODFLG, VEHUPFLG, UPDATFLG, TRACKFLG,
020835,000079: 
020836,000080:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
020837,000081: 
020838,000082:                                                                                                  #        CENTRALS - A,Q,L
020839,000083: 
020840,000084: 25,2062  30,2000                                  SBANK=   LOWSUPER                              #  FOR LOW 2CADR'S.

021255,000499:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021256,000500: 
021257,000501:                                                                                                  #        PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE PROGRAM P25
021258,000502:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 3
021259,000503:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021260,000504: 
021261,000505:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021262,000506: 
021263,000507:                                                                                                  #        THE PURPOSE OF THIS PROGRAM IS TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING
021264,000508:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO CONTINUOUSLY POINT THE LM TRACKING BEACON AT THE
021265,000509:                                                                                                  #        CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE AND
021266,000510:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUSLY MAINTAIN THIS ATTITUDE WITHIN PRESCRIBED LIMITS
021267,000511: 
021268,000512:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021269,000513: 
021270,000514:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT REQUEST THROUGH DSKY V37E25E
021271,000515: 
021272,000516:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021273,000517: 
021274,000518:                                                                                                  #        BANKCALL                                        FLAGUP
021275,000519:                                                                                                  #        R02BOTH (IMU STATUS CHECK)                      ENDOFJOB
021276,000520:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM  (PREF TRK ATT ROUT)                     WAITLIST
021277,000521:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER                                        FINDVAC

021282,000526:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM (P00) BY KEYING V37E00E OR BY KEYING IN V56E

021344,000588:                                                                                                  #  DATA READ ROUTINE 22 (LEM)
021345,000589:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021346,000590: 
021347,000591:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021348,000592:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021349,000593: 
021350,000594:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021351,000595: 
021352,000596:                                                                                                  #        TO PROCESS AUTOMATIC RR MARK DATA TO UPDATE THE STATE VECTOR OF EITHER
021353,000597:                                                                                                  #        LM OR CSM AS DEFINED IN THE RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION PROGRAM (P20)
021354,000598: 
021355,000599:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021356,000600: 
021357,000601:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021358,000602:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R22LEM
021359,000603: 
021360,000604:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021361,000605: 
021362,000606:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.1         GOFLASH         WAITLIST
021363,000607:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.2         PRIOLARM        BANKCALL
021364,000608:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.3         R61LEM
021365,000609: 
021366,000610:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021367,000611: 
021368,000612:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL CONTINUE TO RECYCLE, UPDATING STATE VECTORS WITH RADAR DATA
021369,000613:                                                                                                  #        UNTIL P20 CEASES TO OPERATE (RENDEZVOUS FLAG SET TO ZERO) AT WHICH TIME
021370,000614:                                                                                                  #        R22 WILL TERMINATE SELF.
021371,000615: 
021372,000616:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021373,000617: 
021374,000618:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM
021375,000619:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 525 LOS NOT WITHIN 3 DEGREE LIMIT
021376,000620: 
021377,000621:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021378,000622:

021559,000803:                                                                                                  #  RR DESIGNATE ROUTINE (R21LEM)
021560,000804:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021561,000805: 
021562,000806:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021563,000807:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021564,000808: 
021565,000809:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021566,000810: 
021567,000811:                                                                                                  #        TO POINT THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR AT THE CSM UNTIL AUTOMATIC ACQUISITION
021568,000812:                                                                                                  #        OF THE CSM IS ACCOMPLISHED BY THE RADAR.  ROUTINE IS CALLED BY P20.
021569,000813: 
021570,000814:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021571,000815: 
021572,000816:                                                                                                  #        TC      BANKCALL
021573,000817:                                                                                                  #        CADR    R21LEM
021574,000818: 
021575,000819:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED -
021576,000820: 
021577,000821:                                                                                                  #        FINDVAC         FLAGUP          ENDOFJOB        PRIOLARM
021578,000822:                                                                                                  #        NOVAC           INTPRET         LPS20.1         PHASCHNG
021579,000823:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        JOBSLEEP        JOBWAKE         FLAGDOWN
021580,000824:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER        BANKCALL        RADSTALL        RRDESSM
021581,000825: 
021582,000826:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES
021583,000827:                                                                                                  #        
021584,000828:                                                                                                  #        WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED, BRANCH WILL BE TO P20 WHERE R22 (DATA READ
021585,000829:                                                                                                  #        WILL BE SELECTED OR A NEED FOR A MANEUVER (BRANCH TO P20LEMA)
021586,000830: 
021587,000831:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021588,000832: 
021589,000833:                                                                                                  #        PRIORITY ALARM 503 WHEN LOCK-ON HASN:T BEEN ACHIEVED AFTER 30SECS -
021590,000834:                                                                                                  #        THIS REQUIRES ASTRONAUT INTERFACE- SELECTION OF SEARCH OPTION OF
021591,000835:                                                                                                  #        ACQUISITION
021592,000836: 
021593,000837:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
021594,000838: 
021595,000839:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM
021596,000840: 
021597,000841:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021598,000842: 
021599,000843:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES ARE USED BY LPS20.1 AND RRDESSM
021600,000844: 
021601,000845:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021602,000846: 
021603,000847:                                                                                                  #        LOSCMFLG        LOKONSW
021604,000848: 
021605,000849:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
021606,000850: 
021607,000851:                                                                                                  #        SEE LPS20.1, RRDESSM

021784,001028:                                                                                                  #  MANUAL ACQUISITION ROUTINE R23LEM
021785,001029:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021786,001030: 
021787,001031:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021788,001032:                                                                                                  #        BY P VOLANTE
021789,001033: 
021790,001034:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021791,001035: 
021792,001036:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY MANUAL OPERATION OF THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
021793,001037:

021802,001046: 
021803,001047:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021804,001048: 
021805,001049:                                                                                                  #        IN RESPONSE TO THE GOPERF1      ,SELECTION OF ENTER WILL RECYCLE R23
021806,001050:                                                                                                  #                                        ,SELECTION OF PROC WILL CONTINUE R23

021808,001052:

021868,001112:                                                                                                  #  SEARCH ROUTINE R24LEM
021869,001113:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021870,001114: 
021871,001115:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO - 2
021872,001116:                                                                                                  #        BY P. VOLANTE
021873,001117: 
021874,001118:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
021875,001119: 
021876,001120:                                                                                                  #        TO ACQUIRE THE CSM BY A SEARCH PATTERN WHEN THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR HAS
021877,001121:                                                                                                  #        FAILED TO ACQUIRE THE CSM IN THE AUTOMATIC TRACKING MODE AND TO ALLOW
021878,001122:                                                                                                  #        THE ASTRONAUT TO CONFIRM THAT REACQUISITION HAS NOT BEEN BY SIDELOBE.
021879,001123: 
021880,001124:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
021881,001125: 
021882,001126:                                                                                                  #        CAF     PRIONN
021883,001127:                                                                                                  #        TC      FINDVAC
021884,001128:                                                                                                  #        EBANK=  DATAGOOD
021885,001129:                                                                                                  #        2CADR   R24LEM
021886,001130: 
021887,001131:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
021888,001132: 
021889,001133:                                                                                                  #        FLAGUP          FLAGDOWN        BANKCALL
021890,001134:                                                                                                  #        R61LEM          GOFLASHR        FINDVAC
021891,001135:                                                                                                  #        ENDOFJOB        NOVAC           LSR24.1
021892,001136: 
021893,001137:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT MODES -
021894,001138: 
021895,001139:                                                                                                  #        ASTRONAUT RESPONSE TO DISPLAY OF OMEGA AND DATAGOOD.  HE CAN EITHER
021896,001140:                                                                                                  #        REJECT BY TERMINATING (SEARCH OPTION AND RESELECTING P20) OR ACCEPT BY
021897,001141:                                                                                                  #        PROCEEDING (EXIT ROUTINE AND RETURN TO AUTO MODE IN P20)
021898,001142: 
021899,001143:                                                                                                  #  ALARM OR ABORT EXIT MODES -
021900,001144: 
021901,001145:                                                                                                  #        SEE NORMAL EXIT MODES ABOVE
021902,001146: 
021903,001147:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT -
021904,001148: 
021905,001149:                                                                                                  #        SEE OUTPUT FROM LSR24.1 + R61LEM
021906,001150: 
021907,001151:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
021908,001152: 
021909,001153:                                                                                                  #        SEE INPUT FOR LSR24.1
021910,001154: 
021911,001155:                                                                                                  #  FLAGS SET + RESET
021912,001156: 
021913,001157:                                                                                                  #        SRCHOPT, ACMODFLG
021914,001158: 
021915,001159: 24,3206  E7,1733                                  EBANK=   DATAGOOD                              
021916,001160: 24,3206                                           COUNT*   $$/R24                                
021917,001161: 24,3206           05504        R24LEM             TC       UPFLAG                                
021918,001162: 24,3207           00037                           ADRES    SRCHOPTN                              #  SET SRCHOPT FLAG
021919,001163: 24,3210           05516                           TC       DOWNFLAG                              #  RESET LOS BEING COMPUTED FLAG TO MAKE
021920,001164: 24,3211           00041                           ADRES    LOSCMFLG                              #  SURE DODES DOESN'T GO TO R21
021921,001165: 24,3212           34755        R24LEM1            CAF      ZERO                                  
021922,001166: 24,3213           55733                           TS       DATAGOOD                              #  ZERO OUT DATA INDICATOR

021924,001168: 24,3215           55735                           TS       OMEGAD     +1                         #  ZERO OMEGA DISPLAY REGS

021984,001228:                                                                                                  #  PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE R61LEM
021985,001229:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM DESCRIPTION
021986,001230: 
021987,001231:                                                                                                  #        MOD NO: 3               DATE: 4-11-67
021988,001232:                                                                                                  #        MOD BY: P VOLANTE   SDC
021989,001233: 
021990,001234:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION -
021991,001235: 
021992,001236:                                                                                                  #        TO COMPUTE THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE OF THE LM TO ENABLE RR
021993,001237:                                                                                                  #        TRACKING OF THE CSM AND TO PERFORM THE MANEUVER TO THE PREFERRED
021994,001238:                                                                                                  #        ATTITUDE.
021995,001239: 
021996,001240:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE -
021997,001241:

022193,001437:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ RRLIMCHK                                                        ARE IN THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.
022194,001438: 
022195,001439:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022196,001440: 
022197,001441:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK CHECKS RR DESIRED GIMBAL ANGLES TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN
022198,001442:                                                                                                  #        THE LIMITS OF THE CURRENT MODE.  INITIALLY THE DESIRED TRUNNION AND
022199,001443:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT ANGLES ARE STORED IN ITEMP1 AND ITEMP2.  THE CURRENT RR
022200,001444:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNAE MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED WHICH IS = 0 FOR
022201,001445:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 AND =1 FOR MODE 2.
022202,001446: 
022203,001447:                                                                                                  #        MODE 1 - THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022204,001448:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -55 AND +55 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN LIMITS,
022205,001449:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN -70 AND +59 DEGREES.
022206,001450:                                                                                                  #        IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN TO L +3.
022207,001451: 
022208,001452:                                                                                                  #        MODE 2 - THE SHAFT ANGLE IS CHECKED AT MAGSUB TO SEE IF IT IS
022209,001453:                                                                                                  #        BETWEEN -139 AND -25 DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF WITHIN
022210,001454:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS, THE TRUNNION ANGLE IS CHECKED TO SEE IF IT IS BETWEEN +125
022211,001455:                                                                                                  #        AND -125 (+235) DEGREES.  IF NOT, RETURN TO L +2.  IF IN LIMITS, RETURN
022212,001456:                                                                                                  #        TO L +3.
022213,001457: 
022214,001458:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022215,001459: 
022216,001460:                                                                                                  #        L  TC  RRLIMCHK (WITH INTERRUPT INHIBITED)
022217,001461:                                                                                                  #        L  +1  ADRES  T,S  (DESIRED TRUNNION ANGLE ADDRESS)
022218,001462: 
022219,001463:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022220,001464: 
022221,001465:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, MODEA, MODEB (OR DESIRED TRUNNION AND SHAFT
022222,001466:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES ELSEWHERE IN CONSECUTIVE LOCATIONS - UNSWITCHED ERASABLE OR
022223,001467:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT EBANK).
022224,001468: 
022225,001469:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_   MAGSUB
022226,001470: 
022227,001471:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022228,001472: 
022229,001473:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
022230,001474: 
022231,001475:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         L + 2   (EITHER OR BOTH ANGLES NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022232,001476:                                                                                                  #                L + 3   (BOTH ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE)
022233,001477:

022277,001521:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_ SETTRKF                                                         . IF EITHER:
022278,001522: 
022279,001523:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022280,001524:                                                                                                  #        SETTRKF UPDATES THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP ON THE DSKY.                      HER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION.
022281,001525:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY THE LAMP TEST FLAG (IMODES33 BIT 1) IS CHECKED.
022282,001526:                                                                                                  #        IF A LAMP TEST IS IN PROGRESS, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L +1.
022283,001527:                                                                                                  #        IF NO LAMP TEST THE FOLLOWING IS CHECKED SEQUENTIALLY_
022284,001528:                                                                                                  #                1) RR CDU:S BEING ZEROED, RR CDU OK, AND RR NOT IN
022285,001529:                                                                                                  #                   AUTO MODE (RADMODES BITS 13, 7, 2).
022286,001530:                                                                                                  #                2) LR VEL DATA FAIL AND NO LR POS DATA (RADMODES BITS
022287,001531:                                                                                                  #                   8,5)
022288,001532:                                                                                                  #                3) NO RR DATA (RADMODES BIT 4)
022289,001533:                                                                                                  #        THE ABSENCE OF ALL THREE SIMULTANEOUSLY IN (1), THE PRESENCE OF BOTH
022290,001534:                                                                                                  #        IN (2), AND THE PRESENCE OF (3) RESULTS IN EITHER THE TRACKER FAIL
022291,001535:                                                                                                  #        LAMP (DSPTAB +11D BIT 8) BEING TURNED ON OR LEFT ON. OTHERWISE,
022292,001536:                                                                                                  #        THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED OFF OR IS LEFT OFF. THEREFORE, THE
022293,001537:                                                                                                  #        TRACKER FAIL LAMP IS TURNED ON IF_
022294,001538:                                                                                                  #                A) RR CDU FAILED WITH RR IN AUTO MODE AND RR CDU:S NOT BEING ZEROED.
022295,001539:                                                                                                  #                B) N SAMPLES OF LR DATA COULD NOT BE TAKEN IN 2N TRIES WITH
022296,001540:                                                                                                  #                   EITHER THE ALT OR VEL INFORMATION
022297,001541:                                                                                                  #                C) N SAMPLES OF RR DATA COULD NOT BE OBTAINED FROM 2N TRIES
022298,001542:                                                                                                  #                   WITH EITHER THE AL
022299,001543: 
022300,001544:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022301,001545: 
022302,001546:                                                                                                  #        L       TC      SETTRKF
022303,001547: 
022304,001548:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:  IMODES33, RADMODES, DSPTAB +11D
022305,001549: 
022306,001550:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  NONE
022307,001551: 
022308,001552:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  NONE
022309,001553: 
022310,001554:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL LAMP

022349,001593:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRTURNON
022350,001594: 
022351,001595:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022352,001596: 
022353,001597:                                                                                                  #        RRTURNON IS THE TURN-ON SEQUENCE WHICH, ALONG WITH
022354,001598:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB, ZEROS THE CDU:S AND DETERMINES THE RR MODE.
022355,001599:                                                                                                  #        INITIALLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RRZEROSB FOR THE
022356,001600:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL TURN-ON SEQUENCE.  UPON RETURN THE PROGRAM
022357,001601:                                                                                                  #        WAITS 1 SECOND BEFORE REMOVING THE TURN-ON FLAG
022358,001602:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT1) SO THE REPOSITION ROUTINE WON:T
022359,001603:                                                                                                  #        INITIATE PROGRAM ALARM 00501.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE
022360,001604:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF A PROGRAM IS USING THE RR (STATE BIT 7).  IF
022361,001605:                                                                                                  #        SO, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR SO THAT THE RR CDU
022362,001606:                                                                                                  #        FAIL FLAG (RADMODES BIT 7) CAN BE CHECKED BEFORE
022363,001607:                                                                                                  #        RETURNING TO THE WAITING PROGRAM.  IF NOT, THE PROGRAM EXITS
022364,001608:                                                                                                  #        TO TASKOVER.
022365,001609: 
022366,001610:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  WAITLIST TASK FROM RRAUTCHK IF THE RR POWER ON AUTO
022367,001611:                                                                                                  #  BIT (CHAN 33 BIT 2) CHANGES TO 0 AND NO PROGRAM WAS USING 
022368,001612:                                                                                                  #  THE RR (STATE BIT 7).
022369,001613: 
022370,001614:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022371,001615: 
022372,001616:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES, STATE
022373,001617: 
022374,001618:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  RRZEROSB, FIXDELAY, TASKOVER, ENDRADAR
022375,001619: 
022376,001620:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022377,001621:                                                                                                  #        
022378,001622:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022379,001623: 
022380,001624:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE (SEE RRZEROSB)
022381,001625: 
022382,001626:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, ENDRADAR (WAITING PROGRAM)
022383,001627: 
022384,001628: 24,3255                                           BANK     24                                    
022385,001629: 25,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S1                                 
022386,001630: 25,2000                                           BANK                                           
022387,001631: 
022388,001632: 25,2062  E7,1456                                  EBANK=   LOSCOUNT                              
022389,001633: 25,2062                                           COUNT*   $$/RSUB                               
022390,001634: 25,2062           02071        RRTURNON           TC       RRZEROSB

022398,001642:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRZEROSB
022399,001643: 
022400,001644:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022401,001645:                                                                                                  #        RRZEROSB IS A CLOSED SUBROUTINE TO ZERO THE RR CDU:S,
022402,001646:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINE THE RR MODE, AND TURNS ON THE TRACKER FAIL
022403,001647:                                                                                                  #        LAMP IF REQUIRED.  INITIALLY THE RR CDU ZERO BIT (CHAN 12
022404,001648:                                                                                                  #        BIT 1) IS SET.  FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT, THE LGC
022405,001649:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU COUNTERS (OPTY, OPTX) ARE SET = 0 AFTER 
022406,001650:                                                                                                  #        WHICH THE RR CDU ZERO DISCRETE (CHAN 12 BIT 1) IS
022407,001651:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A 4 SECOND WAIT IS SET TO ALL THE RR CDU:S
022408,001652:                                                                                                  #        TO REPEAT THE ACTUAL TRUNNION AND SHAFT ANGLES.  THE
022409,001653:                                                                                                  #        RR CDU ZERO FLAG (RADMODES BIT 13) IS REMOVED.  THE
022410,001654:                                                                                                  #        CONTENTS OF OPTY IS THEN CHECKED TO SEE IF THE TRUNNION
022411,001655:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE IS LESS THAN 90 DEGREES.  IF NOT, BIT 12 OF
022412,001656:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES IS SET = 1 TO INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 2.
022413,001657:                                                                                                  #        IF LESS THAN 90 DEGREES, BIT 12 OF RADMODES IS SET = 0 TO
022414,001658:                                                                                                  #        INDICATE RR ANTENNA MODE 1.  SETTRKF IS THEN CALLED TO
022415,001659:                                                                                                  #        SEE IF THE TRACKER FAIL LAMP SHOULD BE TURNED ON.
022416,001660: 
022417,001661:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  L  TC  RRZEROSB  (FROM RRTURNON AND RRZERO)
022418,001662: 
022419,001663:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022420,001664: 
022421,001665:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES (BIT 13 SET), DSPTAB +11D
022422,001666: 
022423,001667:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_  FIXDELAY, MAGSUB, SETTRKF
022424,001668: 
022425,001669:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022426,001670: 
022427,001671:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022428,001672: 
022429,001673:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  TRACKER FAIL
022430,001674: 
022431,001675:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  L +1 (ALWAYS)

022436,001680: 25,2074           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  COMING HERE.

022474,001718:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DORREPOS
022475,001719: 
022476,001720:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022477,001721: 
022478,001722:                                                                                                  #        DORREPOS IS A SEQUENCE OF TASKS TO DRIVE THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
022479,001723:                                                                                                  #        TO A SAFE POSITION.  INITIALLY SETRRECR IS CALLED WHERE THE RR
022480,001724:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTERS (CHAN 12 BIT 2) ARE ENABLED AND LASTYCMD
022481,001725:                                                                                                  #        AND LASTXCMD SET = 0 TO INDICATE THE DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE
022482,001726:                                                                                                  #        DESIRED STATE AND PRESENT STATE OF THE COMMANDS.  THE RR
022483,001727:                                                                                                  #        TURN-ON FLAG (RADMODES BIT 1) IS CHECKED AND IF NOT PRESENT,
022484,001728:                                                                                                  #        PROGRAM ALARM 00501 IS REQUESTED BEFORE CONTINUING.  IN EITHER
022485,001729:                                                                                                  #        CASE, FOLLOWING A 20 MILLISECOND WAIT THE PROGRAM CHECKS THE CURRENT
022486,001730:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE (RADMODES BIT 12).  RRTONLY IS THEN CALLED
022487,001731:                                                                                                  #        TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO 180
022488,001732:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  UPON RETURN, THE CURRENT RR ANTENNA
022489,001733:                                                                                                  #        MODE (RADMODES BIT 12) IS AGAIN CHECKED.  RRSONLY IS THEN
022490,001734:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO DRIVE THE SHAFT ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1 AND TO
022491,001735:                                                                                                  #        -90 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  IF DURING RRTONLY OR RRSONLY A
022492,001736:                                                                                                  #        REMODE HAS BEEN REQUESTED (RADMODES BIT 14), AND ALWAYS
022493,001737:                                                                                                  #        FOLLOWING COMPLETION OF RRSONLY, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO
022494,001738:                                                                                                  #        REPOSRPT.  HERE THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS 
022495,001739:                                                                                                  #        REMOVED.  A CHECK IS THEN MADE ON THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
022496,001740:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10).  IF PRESENT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO BEGDES.  IF NOT PRESENT
022497,001741:                                                                                                  #        INDICATING NO FURTHER ANTENNA CONTROL REQUIRED, THE RR ERROR
022498,001742:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS REMOVED AND THE ROUTINE EXITS TO
022499,001743:                                                                                                  #        TASKOVER.
022500,001744: 
022501,001745:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022502,001746: 
022503,001747:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM RRGIMON IF TRUNNION AND SHAFT CDU ANGLES
022504,001748:                                                                                                  #        NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF CURRENT MODE.
022505,001749: 
022506,001750:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022507,001751: 
022508,001752:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022509,001753: 
022510,001754:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022511,001755: 
022512,001756:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, BEGDES (EXIT)
022513,001757: 
022514,001758:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_
022515,001759: 
022516,001760:                                                                                                  #        NONE
022517,001761: 
022518,001762:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS-  NONE
022519,001763: 
022520,001764:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_  TASKOVER, BEGDES

022567,001811:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  REMODE                                                         IVES SHAFT TO -45, AND FINALLY DRIVES
022568,001812: 
022569,001813:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       S DONE WITH SINGLE AXIS ROTATIONS (SEE
022570,001814:                                                                                                  #        REMODE IS THE GENERAL REMODING SUBROUTINE.  IT DRIVES THE
022571,001815:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF THE CURRENT MODE IS MODE 1,
022572,001816:                                                                                                  #        180 DEGREES FOR MODE 2, THEN DRIVES THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45
022573,001817:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES, AND FINALLY DRIVES THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130 DEGREES,
022574,001818:                                                                                                  #        TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2, -50 DEGREES FOR MODE 1, BEFORE
022575,001819:                                                                                                  #        INITIATING 2-AXIS CONTROL.  ALL REMODING IS DONE WITH SINGLE
022576,001820:                                                                                                  #        AXIS ROTATIONS (RR1AXIS).  INITIALLY THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022577,001821:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED.  CONTROL IS THEN TRANSFERRED TO
022578,001822:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY TO DRIVE THR TRUNNION ANGLE TO 0 DEGREES IF IN MODE 1
022579,001823:                                                                                                  #        OR 180 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2.  RRSONLY IS THEN CALLED TO DRIVE
022580,001824:                                                                                                  #        THE SHAFT ANGLE TO -45 DEGREES. THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG
022581,001825:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) IS CHECKED AGAIN.  CONTROL IS AGAIN
022582,001826:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RRTONLY TO DRIVE THE TRUNNION ANGLE TO -130
022583,001827:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 2 IF CURRENTLY IN MODE 1 OR TO
022584,001828:                                                                                                  #        -50 DEGREES IF IN MODE 2 TO PLACE THE RR IN MODE 1.  RMODINV
022585,001829:                                                                                                  #        IS THEN CALLED TO SET RADMODES BIT 12 TO INDICATE THE NEW
022586,001830:                                                                                                  #        RR ANTENNA MODE.  THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14)
022587,001831:                                                                                                  #        IS REMOVED TO INDICATE THAT REMODING IS COMPLETE.  THE PROGRAM
022588,001832:                                                                                                  #        THEN EXITS TO STDESIG TO BEGIN 2-AXIS CONTROL.
022589,001833: 
022590,001834:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022591,001835: 
022592,001836:                                                                                                  #        FROM BEGDES WHEN REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) IS SET.
022593,001837:                                                                                                  #        THIS FLAG MAY BE SET IN RRDESSM AND RRDESNB IF RRLIMCHK
022594,001838:                                                                                                  #        DETERMINES THAT THE DESIRED ANGLES ARE WITHIN THE LIMITS OF THE
022595,001839:                                                                                                  #        OTHER MODE.
022596,001840: 
022597,001841:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022598,001842: 
022599,001843:                                                                                                  #        RADMODES
022600,001844: 
022601,001845:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
022602,001846:

022604,001848:

022606,001850:

022664,001908:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAMES_        RRTONLY, RRSONLY
022665,001909: 
022666,001910:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022667,001911: 
022668,001912:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE SUBROUTINES FOR DOING SINGLE AXIS
022669,001913:                                                                                                  #        RR MANEUVERS FOR REMODE AND REPOSITION.  IT DRIVES TO
022670,001914:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  INITIALLY, AT RR1AX2, THE REMODE AND REPOSITION
022671,001915:                                                                                                  #        FLAGS (RADMODES BITS 14, 11) ARE CHECKED.  IF BOTH EXIST,
022672,001916:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO REPOSRPT (SEE DORREPOS).  THIS INDICATES
022673,001917:                                                                                                  #        THAT SOMEONE POSSIBLY REQUESTED A DESIGNATE (RADMODES BIT 10)
022674,001918:                                                                                                  #        WHICH REQUIRES A REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) AND THAT A
022675,001919:                                                                                                  #        REPOSITION IS IN PROGRESS (RADMODES BIT 11).  IF NONE
022676,001920:                                                                                                  #        OR ONLY ONE OF THE FLAGS EXIST, REMODE OR REPOSITION, MAGSUB
022677,001921:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE APPROPRIATE ANGLE IS WITHIN 1 DEGREE.  IF YES,
022678,001922:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL RETURNS TO THE CALLING ROUTINE.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS
022679,001923:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO RROUT FOR SINGLE AXIS MANEUVERS WITH THE OTHER
022680,001924:                                                                                                  #        ANGLE SET = 0.  FOLLOWING A .5 SECOND WAIT, THE ABOVE PROCEDURE IS
022681,001925:                                                                                                  #        REPEATED.
022682,001926: 
022683,001927:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:     L-1     CAF     *ANGLE*         (DESIRED ANGLE SCALED PI)
022684,001928:                                                                                                  #                        L       TC      RRTONLY         (TRUNNION ONLY)
022685,001929:                                                                                                  #                        RRSONLY                         (SHAFT ONLY)
022686,001930:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY IS CALLED BY PREPOS29;
022687,001931:                                                                                                  #                        RRTONLY AND RRSONLY ARE CALLED BY DORREPOS AND REMODE
022688,001932: 
022689,001933:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022690,001934: 
022691,001935:                                                                                                  #        C(A) = DESIRED ANGLE, RADMODES
022692,001936:

022694,001938:

022704,001948:                                                                                                  #        BITS 14, 11)

022757,002001:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RROUT                                                          RROR COUNTER SCALING. RROUT LIMITS THEM
022758,002002: 
022759,002003:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022760,002004: 
022761,002005:                                                                                                  #        RROUT RECEIVES RR GYRO COMMANDS IN TANG, TANG +1 IN RR
022762,002006:                                                                                                  #        ERROR COUNTER SCALING.  RROUT THEN LIMITS THEM AND
022763,002007:                                                                                                  #        GENERATES COMMANDS TO THE CDU TO ADJUST THE ERROR COUNTERS
022764,002008:                                                                                                  #        TO THE DESIRED VALUES.  INITIALLY MAGSUB CHECKS THE MAGNITUDE OF
022765,002009:                                                                                                  #        THE COMMAND (SHAFT ON 1ST PASS) TO SEE IF IT IS GREATER THAN
022766,002010:                                                                                                  #        384 PULSES.  IF NOT, CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO RROUTLIM TO
022767,002011:                                                                                                  #        LIMIT THE COMMAND TO +384 OR -384 PULSES.  THE DIFFERENCE IS
022768,002012:                                                                                                  #        THEN CALCULATED BETWEEN THE DESIRED STATE AND THE PRESENT STATE OF
022769,002013:                                                                                                  #        THE ERROR COUNTER AS RECORDED IN LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD.
022770,002014:                                                                                                  #        THE RESULT IS STORED IN OPTXCMD (1ST PASS) AND OPTYCMD (2ND
022771,002015:                                                                                                  #        PASS).  FOLLOWING THE SECOND PASS, FOR THE TRUNNION COMMAND, THE
022772,002016:                                                                                                  #        OCDUT AND OCDUS ERROR COUNTER DRIVE BITS (CHAN 14 BITS 12, 11)
022773,002017:                                                                                                  #        ARE SET.  THIS PROGRAM THEN EXITS TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022774,002018: 
022775,002019:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022776,002020:                                                                                                  #

022778,002022:                                                                                                  #        RRTONLY, RRSONLY, AND DODES

022867,002111:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  RRDESSM                                                        R (HALF-UNIT) IN RRTARGET. REMODES IF
022868,002112: 
022869,002113:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
022870,002114: 
022871,002115:                                                                                                  #        THIS INTERPRETIVE ROUTINE WILL DESIGNATE, IF DESIRED ANGLES ARE
022872,002116:                                                                                                  #        WITHIN THE LIMITS OF EITHER MODE, TO A LINE-OF SIGHT (LOS) VECTOR
022873,002117:                                                                                                  #        (HALF-UNIT) KNOWN WITH RESPECT TO THE STABLE MEMBER PRESENT
022874,002118:                                                                                                  #        ORIENTATION.  INITIALLY THE IMU CDU:S ARE READ AND CONTROL
022875,002119:                                                                                                  #        TRANSFERRED TO SMNB TO TRANSFORM THE LOS VECTOR FROM STABLE
022876,002120:                                                                                                  #        MEMBER TO NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES (SEE STG MEMO -699)
022877,002121:                                                                                                  #        RRANGLES IS THEN CALLED TO CALCULATE THE RR GIMBAL ANGLES,
022878,002122:                                                                                                  #        TRUNNION AND SHAFT, FOR BOTH THE PRESENT AND ALTERNATE MODE.
022879,002123:                                                                                                  #        RRLIMCHK IS CALLED TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE
022880,002124:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT MODE ARE WITHIN LIMITS.  IF WITHIN LIMITS, THE RETURN
022881,002125:                                                                                                  #        LOCATION IS INCREMENTED, INASMUCH AS NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS
022882,002126:                                                                                                  #        REQUIRED, BEFORE EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF NOT WITHIN LIMITS OF THE
022883,002127:                                                                                                  #        CURRENT MODE, TRYSWS IS CALLED.  FOLLOWING INVERTING OF THE RR
022884,002128:                                                                                                  #        ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 12), RRLIMCHK IS CALLED
022885,002129:                                                                                                  #        TO SEE IF THE ANGLES CALCULATED FOR THE ALTERNATE MODE ARE WITHIN
022886,002130:                                                                                                  #        LIMITS.  IF YES, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG IS AGAIN INVERTED,
022887,002131:                                                                                                  #        THE REMODE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 14) SET, AND THE RETURN LOCATION
022888,002132:                                                                                                  #        INCREMENTED, TO INDICATE NO VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED, BEFORE
022889,002133:                                                                                                  #        EXITING TO STARTDES.  IF THESE ANGLES ARE NOT WITHIN LIMITS
022890,002134:                                                                                                  #        OF THE ALTERNATE MODE, THE RR ANTENNA MODE FLAG (RADMODES
022891,002135:                                                                                                  #        BIT 12) IS INVERTED BEFORE RETURNING DIRECTLY TO THE CALLING PROGRAM
022892,002136:                                                                                                  #        TO INDICATE THAT A VEHICLE MANEUVER IS REQUIRED.
022893,002137: 
022894,002138:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
022895,002139: 
022896,002140:                                                                                                  #        L       STCALL  RRTARGET        (LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN SM COORDINATES)
022897,002141:                                                                                                  #        L+1     RRDESSM
022898,002142:                                                                                                  #        L+2     BASIC                   (VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022899,002143:                                                                                                  #        L+3     BASIC                   (NO VEHICLE MANEUVER REQUIRED)
022900,002144: 
022901,002145:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
022902,002146: 
022903,002147:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET, RADMODES
022904,002148:

022906,002150:

022908,002152:                                                                                                  #        PART OF), RMODINV
022909,002153:

022911,002155:

022957,002201:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  STARTDES                                                       STORED AS A HALF-UNIT VECTOR IN RRTARGET
022958,002202: 
022959,002203:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_                                                       CKON IS DESIRED. BIT14 OF RADMODES IS
022960,002204:                                                                                                  #        STARTDES IS ENTERED WHEN WE ARE READY TO BEGIN DESIGNATION.             OR REPOSITION OPERATION. IN THIS
022961,002205:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14 OF RADMODES IS ALREADY SET IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED.              THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022962,002206:                                                                                                  #        AT THIS TIME, THE RR ANTENNA MAY BE IN A REPOSITION                     GINS.
022963,002207:                                                                                                  #        OPERATION.  IN THIS CASE, IF A REMODE IS REQUIRED IT MAY HAVE
022964,002208:                                                                                                  #        ALREADY BEGUN BUT IN ANY CASE THE REPOSITION WILL BE INTERRUPTED.
022965,002209:                                                                                                  #        OTHERWISE, THE REPOSITION WILL BE COMPLETED BEFORE 2-AXIS
022966,002210:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATION BEGINS.  INITIALLY DESCOUNT IS SET = 60 TO INDICATE
022967,002211:                                                                                                  #        THAT 30 SECONDS WILL BE ALLOWED FOR THE RR DATA GOOD INBIT
022968,002212:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 33 BIT 4) IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED (STATE BIT 5).  BIT 10
022969,002213:                                                                                                  #        OF RADMODES IS SET TO SHOW THAT A DESIGNATE IS REQUIRED.
022970,002214:                                                                                                  #        THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF SET,
022971,002215:                                                                                                  #        THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM (SEE RRDESSM
022972,002216:                                                                                                  #        AND RRDESNB).  THE PROGRAM WILL BEGIN DESIGNATING TO THE DESIRED
022973,002217:                                                                                                  #        ANGLES FOLLOWING THE REPOSITION OR REMODE IF ONE WAS
022974,002218:                                                                                                  #        REQUESTED.  IF THE REPOSITION FLAG IS NOT SET, SETRRECR IS CALLED
022975,002219:                                                                                                  #        WHICH SETS THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2)
022976,002220:                                                                                                  #        AND SETS LASTYCMD AND LASTXCMD = 0 TO INDICATE THE
022977,002221:                                                                                                  #        DIFFERENCE BETWEEN THE PRESENT AND DESIRED STATE OF THE ERROR
022978,002222:                                                                                                  #        COUNTERS.  A 20 MILLISECOND WAITLIST CALL IS SET FOR BEGDES
022979,002223:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO L+3 OF THE CALLING PROGRAM.
022980,002224:

022982,002226: 
022983,002227:                                                                                                  #        FROM RRDESSM AND RRDESNB WHEN ANGLES WITHIN LIMITS.
