023130,002374:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  BEGDES
023131,002375: 
023132,002376:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023133,002377: 
023134,002378:                                                                                                  #        BEGDES CHECKS VARIOUS DESIGNATE REQUESTS AND REQUESTS THE
023135,002379:                                                                                                  #        ACTUAL RR DESIGNATION.  INITIALLY A CHECK IS MADE TO SEE IF A
023136,002380:                                                                                                  #        REMODE (RADMODES BIT 14) IS REQUESTED OR IN PROGRESS.  IF SO,
023137,002381:                                                                                                  #        CONTROL IS TRANSFERRED TO STDESIG AFTER ROUTINE REMODE IS
023138,002382:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTED.  IF NO REMODE, STDESIG IS IMMEDIATELY CALLED WHERE
023139,002383:                                                                                                  #        FIRST THE REPOSITION FLAG (RADMODES BIT 11) IS CHECKED.  IF
023140,002384:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS REMOVED
023141,002385:                                                                                                  #        AFTER WHICH THE PROGRAM EXITS TO RDBADEND.  IF THE REPOSITION
023142,002386:                                                                                                  #        FLAG IS NOT PRESENT, THE CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023143,002387:                                                                                                  #        BIT 15) IS CHECKED.  IF PRESENT, ON EXECUTIVE CALL IS IMMEDIATELY
023144,002388:                                                                                                  #        MADE FOR DODES AFTER WHICH A .5 SECOND WAIT IS INITIATED BEFORE
023145,002389:                                                                                                  #        REPEATING AT STDESIG.  IF THE RR SEARCH ROUTINE (LRS24.1) IS DESIGNATING
023146,002390:                                                                                                  #        TO A NEW POINT (NEWPTFLG SET) THE CURRENT DESIGNATE TASK IS TERMINATED.
023147,002391:                                                                                                  #        IF CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE IS NOT WANTED, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES
023148,002392:                                                                                                  #        BIT 10) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE PROGRAM EXITS TO ENDRADAR TO
023149,002393:                                                                                                  #        CHECK RR CDU FAIL BEFORE RETURNING TO THE CALLING PROGRAM.  IF DESIGNATE
023150,002394:                                                                                                  #        IS STILL REQUIRED, DESCOUNT IS CHECKED TO SEE IF THE 30 SECONDS HAS
023151,002395:                                                                                                  #        EXPIRED BEFORE RECEIVING THE RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4)
023152,002396:                                                                                                  #        SIGNAL.  IF OUT OF TIME, PROGRAM ALARM 00503 IS REQUESTED, THE
023153,002397:                                                                                                  #        RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE AND RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE
023154,002398:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BITS 14,2) BITS REMOVED, AND THE DESIGNATE FLAG
023155,002399:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 10) REMOVED BEFORE EXITING TO RDBADEND.  IF
023156,002400:                                                                                                  #        TIME HAS NOT EXPIRED, DESCOUNT IS DECREMENTED, THE
023157,002401:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL MADE FOR DODES, AND A .5 SECOND WAIT INITIATED
023158,002402:                                                                                                  #        BEFORE REPEATING THIS PROCEDURE AT STDESIG.
023159,002403: 
023160,002404:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023161,002405: 
023162,002406:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST CALL FROM STARTDES
023163,002407:                                                                                                  #        TCF BEGDES FROM DORREPOS
023164,002408:                                                                                                  #        TC STDESIG RETURNING, FROM REMODE
023165,002409: 
023166,002410:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023167,002411:                                                                                                  #        DESCOUNT, RADMODES
023168,002412: 
023169,002413:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023170,002414:                                                                                                  #        ENDRADAR, FINDVAC
023171,002415: 
023172,002416:                                                                                                  #  JOBS OR TASKS INITIATED_  DODES
023173,002417: 
023174,002418:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  PROGRAM ALARM 00503 (30 SECONDS HAVE EXPIRED) WITH NO RR DATA
023175,002419:                                                                                                  #  GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) RECEIVED WHEN LOCK-ON (STATE BIT 5) WAS REQUESTED.
023176,002420: 
023177,002421:                                                                                                  #  EXIT_         TASKOVER (SEARCH PATTERN DESIGNATING TO NEW POINT)
023178,002422:                                                                                                  #                ENDRADAR (NO DESIGNATE - RADMODES BIT 10)
023179,002423:                                                                                                  #                RDBADEND (REPOSITION OR 30 SECONDS EXPIRED)
023180,002424: 
023181,002425: 25,2573           40110        BEGDES             CS       RADMODES

023225,002469:

Page 547 

023227,002471:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  DODES
023228,002472: 
023229,002473:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023230,002474: 
023231,002475:                                                                                                  #        DODES CALCULATES AND REQUESTS ISSUANCE OF RR GYRO TORQUE
023232,002476:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS.  INITIALLY THE CURRENT RR CDU ANGLES ARE STORED AND
023233,002477:                                                                                                  #        THE LOS HALF-UNIT VECTOR TRANSFORMED FROM STABLE MEMBER TO
023234,002478:                                                                                                  #        NAVIGATION BASE COORDINATES VIA SMNB IF NECESSARY.  THE
023235,002479:                                                                                                  #        SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS ARE THEN CALCULATED AS FOLLOWS_
023236,002480:                                                                                                  #                + SHAFT = LOS . (COS(S), 0, -SIN(S))  (DOT PRODUCT)
023237,002481:                                                                                                  #                - TRUNNION = LOS . (SIN(T)SIN(S), COS(T), SIN(T)COS(S))
023238,002482:                                                                                                  #        THE SIGN OF THE SHAFT COMMAND IS THEN REVERSED IF IN MODE 2
023239,002483:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 12) BECAUSE A RELAY IN THE RR REVERSES THE 
023240,002484:                                                                                                  #        POLARITY OF THE COMMAND.  AT RRSCALUP EACH COMMAND IS
023241,002485:                                                                                                  #        SCALED AND IF EITHER, OR BOTH, OF THE COMMANDS IS GREATER THAN
023242,002486:                                                                                                  #        .5 DEGREES, MPAC +1 IS SET POSITIVE.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE 
023243,002487:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 15) IS DESIRED AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS NOT OPERATING,
023244,002488:                                                                                                  #        THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT
023245,002489:                                                                                                  #        CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11)
023246,002490:                                                                                                  #        IS IN PROGRESS.  IF A CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND THE SEARCH ROUTINE IS
023247,002491:                                                                                                  #        OPERATING (SRCHOPT FLAG SET) THE TRACK ENABLE IS NOT CLEARED.  IF NO
023248,002492:                                                                                                  #        CONTINUOUS DESIGNATE AND BOTH COMMANDS ARE NOT LESS THAN .5 DEGREES AS
023249,002493:                                                                                                  #        INDICATED BY MPAC +1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS
023250,002494:                                                                                                  #        CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023251,002495:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5
023252,002496:                                                                                                  #        DEGREES AS INDICATED BY MPAC+1, THE RR AUTO TRACKER ENABLE BIT
023253,002497:                                                                                                  #        (CHAN 12 BIT 14) IS CLEARED AND RROUT CALLED TO PUT OUT THE
023254,002498:                                                                                                  #        COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN
023255,002499:                                                                                                  #        PROGRESS.  IF BOTH COMMANDS ARE LESS THAN .5 DEGREES, THE
023256,002500:                                                                                                  #        LOCK-ON FLAG (STATE BIT 5) IS CHECKED.  IF NOT PRESENT, THE
023257,002501:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED, THE RR ERROR
023258,002502:                                                                                                  #        COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED, AND ENDOFJOB
023259,002503:                                                                                                  #        CALLED. IF LOCK-ON IS DESIRED, THE RR AUTO TRACKER (CHAN 12
023260,002504:                                                                                                  #        BIT 14) IS ENABLED FOLLOWED BY A CHECK OF THE RECEIPT OF THE
023261,002505:                                                                                                  #        RR DATA GOOD (CHAN 33 BIT 4) SIGNAL.  IF RR DATA GOOD
023262,002506:                                                                                                  #        PRESENT, THE DESIGNATE FLAG (RADMODES BIT 10) IS CLEARED,
023263,002507:                                                                                                  #        THE RR ERROR COUNTER ENABLE BIT (CHAN 12 BIT 2) IS CLEARED,
023264,002508:                                                                                                  #        AND ENDOFJOB CALLED.  IF RR DATA GOOD IS NOT PRESENT, RROUT
023265,002509:                                                                                                  #        IS CALLED TO PUT OUT THE COMMANDS PROVIDED NO REPOSITION
023266,002510:                                                                                                  #        (RADMODES BIT 11) IS IN PROGRESS AFTER WHICH THE JOB IS TERMINATED
023267,002511:                                                                                                  #        VIA ENDOFJOB.
023268,002512: 
023269,002513:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:
023270,002514: 
023271,002515:                                                                                                  #        EXECUTIVE CALL EVERY .5 SECONDS FROM BEGDES.
023272,002516: 
023273,002517:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
023274,002518: 
023275,002519:                                                                                                  #        RRTARGET (HALF-UNIT LOS VECTOR IN EITHER SM OR NB COORDINATES),
023276,002520:                                                                                                  #        LOKONSW (STATE BIT 5), RRNBSW (STATE BIT 6), RADMODES
023277,002521:

023345,002589:                                                                                                  #  AT THIS POINT WE HAVE A ROTATION VECTOR IN DISH AXES LYING IN THE TS PLANE.  CONVERT THIS TO A

023353,002597: 25,2722           74740                           MASK     BIT12                                 #  THE SHAFT COMMANDS IN MODE 2 SO THAT A
023354,002598: 25,2723           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  POSITIVE TORQUE APPLIED TO THE SHAFT

023356,002600: 25,2725           31110                           CA       TANG       +1                         #  SHAFT ANGLE.  COMPENSATE FOR THIS SWITCH

023896,003140:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME_  LPS20.1 VECTOR EXTRAPOLATION AND LOS COMPUTATION
023897,003141:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO. 2    BY J.D. COYNE   SDC     DATE 12-7-66
023898,003142: 
023899,003143:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION_
023900,003144:                                                                                                  #        1)      EXTRAPOLATE THE LEM AND CSM VECTORS IN ACCORDANCE WITH THE TIME REFERED TO IN CALLER + 1.
023901,003145:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPUTES THE LOS VECTOR TO THE CSM, CONVERTS IT TO STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES AND STORES IT IN RRTARGET.
023902,003146:                                                                                                  #        3)      COMPUTES THE MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR AND STORES IT IN MLOSV
023903,003147: 
023904,003148:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE      CALL
023905,003149:                                                                                                  #                                LPS20.1
023906,003150: 
023907,003151:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED_
023908,003152:                                                                                                  #        LEMPREC, CSMPREC
023909,003153: 
023910,003154:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT_  RETURN TO CALLER + 2
023911,003155: 
023912,003156:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS_  NONE
023913,003157: 
023914,003158:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS_  NONE
023915,003159: 
023916,003160:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT_
023917,003161:                                                                                                  #        LOS VECTOR (HALF UNIT) IN SM COORDINATES STORED IN RRTARGET
023918,003162:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF THE LOS VECTOR (METERS SCALED B-29) STORED IN MSLOV
023919,003163:                                                                                                  #        RRNBSW CLEARED
023920,003164: 
023921,003165:                                                                                                  #  INITIALIZED ERASEABLE
023922,003166:                                                                                                  #        TDEC1 MUST CONTAIN THE TIME FOR EXTRAPOLATION
023923,003167:                                                                                                  #        SEE ORBITAL INTEGRATION ROUTINE
023924,003168: 
023925,003169:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS_
023926,003170:                                                                                                  #        MPAC DESTROYED BY THIS ROUTINE
023927,003171: 
023928,003172: 23,2314                                           BANK     23                                    
023929,003173: 24,2000                                           SETLOC   P20S                                  
023930,003174: 24,2000                                           BANK

Page 565 

023932,003176: 24,3255                                           COUNT*   $$/LPS20                              
023933,003177: 
023934,003178: 24,3255           43020        LPS20.1            STQ      BOFF                                  
023935,003179: 24,3256           01757                                    LS21X                                 
023936,003180: 24,3257           01343                                    LOSCMFLG                              #  LOSCMFLG = 0 MEANS NOT CALLED BY R21
023937,003181: 24,3260           51264                                    LMINT                                 #  SO CALL LEMCONIC TO GET LM STATE
023938,003182: 24,3261           77614                           BON                                            #  IF IN R21 AND ON LUNAR SURFACE
023939,003183: 24,3262           04307                                    SURFFLAG                              #  DON'T CALL LEMCONIC
023940,003184: 24,3263           51274                                    CSMINT                                
023941,003185: 24,3264           77624        LMINT              CALL                                           
023942,003186: 24,3265           27100                                    LEMCONIC                              #  EXTRAPOLATE LEM
023943,003187: 24,3266           77775                           VLOAD

024025,003269:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME:  LRS22.1 (DATA READ SUBROUTINE 1)
024026,003270:                                                                                                  #  MOD. NO.: 1           BY: P. VOLANTE  SDC             DATE:  11-15-66
024027,003271: 
024028,003272:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024029,003273:                                                                                                  #        1)      READS RENDEZVOUS RADAR RANGE AND RANGE-RATE, TRUNION AND SHAFT ANGLES, THREE CDU VALUES AND TIME.  CONVERTS THIS
024030,003274:                                                                                                  #                DATA AND LEAVES IT FOR THE MEASUREMENT INCORPORATION ROUTINE (LSR22.3).  CHECKS FOR THE RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE, FOR
024031,003275:                                                                                                  #                RR REPOSITION AND RR CDU FAIL
024032,003276:                                                                                                  #        2)      COMPARES RADAR LOS WITH LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS TO SEE IF THEY ARE WITHIN THREE DEGREES
024033,003277: 
024034,003278:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BANKCALL FOR LRS22.1
024035,003279: 
024036,003280:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
024037,003281:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          LPS20.1
024038,003282:                                                                                                  #        RRRANGE         BANKCALL
024039,003283:                                                                                                  #        RADSTALL        CDULOGIC
024040,003284:                                                                                                  #        RRNB            SMNB
024041,003285: 
024042,003286:                                                                                                  #  NORMAL EXIT:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH MPAC SET TO +0
024043,003287: 
024044,003288:                                                                                                  #  ERROR EXITS:  RETURN TO CALLER+1 WITH ERROR CODE STORED IN MPAC AS FOLLOWS:
024045,003289:                                                                                                  #        00001 - ERROR EXIT 1 - RR DATA NO GOOD (NO RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE OR RR CDU FAIL OR RR REPOSITION)
024046,003290:                                                                                                  #        00002 - ERROR EXIT 2 - RR LOS NOT WITHIN THREE DEGREES OF LOS COMPUTED FROM STATE VECTORS
024047,003291: 
024048,003292:                                                                                                  #  ALARMS:  521 - COULD NOT READ RADAR DATA (RR DATA GOOD DISCRETE NOT PRESENT BEFORE AND AFTER READING THE RADAR)
024049,003293:                                                                                                  #        (THIS ALARM IS ISSUED BY THE RADAREAD SUBROUTINE WHICH IS ENTERED FROM A RADARUPT)
024050,003294: 
024051,003295:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  RRLOSVEC - THE RR LINE-OF-SIGHT VECTOR (USED BY LRS22.2) - A HALF-UNIT VECTOR
024052,003296:                                                                                                  #        RM - THE RR RANGE READING (TO THE CSM) DP, IN METERS SCALED B-29 (USED BY LRS22.2 AND LRS22.3)
024053,003297: 
024054,003298:                                                                                                  #        ALL OF THE FOLLOWING OUTPUTS ARE USED BY LRS22.3:
024055,003299:                                                                                                  #                RDOTM - THE RR RANGE-RATE READING, DP, IN METERS PER CENTISECOND, SCALED B-7
024056,003300:                                                                                                  #                RRTRUN - RR TRUNION ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024057,003301:                                                                                                  #                RRSHAFT - RR SHAFT ANGLE, DP, IN REVOLUTIONS, SCALED B0
024058,003302:                                                                                                  #                AIG,AMG,AOG - THE CDU ANGLES, THREE SP WORDS
024059,003303:                                                                                                  #                MKTIME - THE TIME OF THE RR READING, DP, IN CENTISECONDS
024060,003304: 
024061,003305:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
024062,003306:                                                                                                  #        RNRAD, THE RADAR READ COUNTER FROM WHICH IS OBTAINED:

Page 569

024065,003309:                                                                                                  #                2) RR RANGE RATE, SCALED .6278 FT./SEC. PER BIT
024066,003310:                                                                                                  #        THE CDU ANGLES FROM CDUX, CDUY, CDUZ AND TIME1 AND TIME2
024067,003311:

024252,003496: 
024253,003497:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024254,003498:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR EACH OF THE QUANTITIES MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS
024255,003499:                                                                                                  #        RADAR.  (RANGE, RANGE RATE, SHAFT AND TRUNNION ANGLES).  THE ROUTINE CALLS THE INCORP1 AND INCORP2 ROUTINES
024256,003500:                                                                                                  #        WHICH COMPUTE THE DEVIATIONS AND CORRECT THE STATE VECTOR.
024257,003501: 
024258,003502:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE
024259,003503:                                                                                                  #        THIS ROUTINE IS PART OF P20 RENDEZVOUS NAVIGATION FOR THE LM COMPUTER ONLY.  THE ROUTINE IS ENTERED FROM
024260,003504:                                                                                                  #        R22 LEM ONLY AND RETURNS DIRECTLY TO R22LEM FOLLOWING SUCCESSFUL INCORPORATION OF MEASURED DATA.  IF THE
024261,003505:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTED STATE VECTOR DEVIATIONS EXCEED THE MAXIMUM PERMITTED.  THE ROUTINE RETURNS TO R22LEM TO DISPLAY
024262,003506:                                                                                                  #        THE DEVIATIONS.  IF THE ASTRONAUT ACCEPTS THE DATA R22LEM RETURNS TO LSR22.3 TO INCORPORATE THE
024263,003507:                                                                                                  #        DEVIATIONS INTO THE STATE VECTOR.  IF THE ASTRONAUT REJECTS THE DEVIATIONS, NO MORE MEASUREMENTS ARE
024264,003508:                                                                                                  #        PROCESSED FOR THIS MARK, I.E.,  R22LEM GETS THE NEXT MARK.
024265,003509: 
024266,003510:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024267,003511:                                                                                                  #        WLINIT          LGCUPDTE        INTEGRV         INCORP1         ARCTAN
024268,003512:                                                                                                  #        GETULC          RARARANG        INCORP2         NBSM            INTSTALL
024269,003513: 
024270,003514:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024271,003515:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED LM OR CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024272,003516:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR
024273,003517:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP METERS B-29
024274,003518:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024275,003519:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024276,003520: 
024277,003521:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024278,003522:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024279,003523:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024280,003524:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024281,003525:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024282,003526:                                                                                                  #                RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSES B-7
024283,003527:                                                                                                  #                SHAFT ANGLE IN RRSHAFT REVS. B0
024284,003528:                                                                                                  #                TRUNNION ANGLE IN RRTRUN REVS. B0
024285,003529:                                                                                                  #        GIMBAL ANGLES   INNER IN AIG
024286,003530:                                                                                                  #                        MIDDLE IN AMG
024287,003531:                                                                                                  #                        OUTER IN AOG
024288,003532:                                                                                                  #        REFSMMAT
024289,003533:                                                                                                  #        RENDWFLG
024290,003534:                                                                                                  #        NOANGFLG
024291,003535:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024292,003536: 
024293,003537:                                                                                                  #  DEBRIS
024294,003538:                                                                                                  #        PUSHLIST -- ALL
024295,003539:                                                                                                  #        MX, MY, MZ (VECTORS)

Page 575 

024297,003541:                                                                                                  #        ULC, RXZ, SINTHETA, LGRET, RDRET, BVECTOR, W.IND, X78T
024298,003542: 
024299,003543: 13,2207                                           BANK     13

024690,003934: 
024691,003935:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024692,003936:                                                                                                  #        LSR22.4 IS THE ENTRY TO PERFORM LUNAR SURFACE NAVIGATION FOR THE LM
024693,003937:                                                                                                  #        COMPUTER ONLY.  THIS ROUTINE COMPUTES THE B-VECTORS AND DELTA Q FOR RANGE
024694,003938:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE MEASURED BY THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR
024695,003939: 
024696,003940:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED
024697,003941:                                                                                                  #        INSTALL         LGCUPDTE        INCORP1         RP-TO-R
024698,003942:                                                                                                  #        INTEGRV         GETULC          INCORP2
024699,003943: 
024700,003944:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT
024701,003945:                                                                                                  #        CORRECTED CSM STATE VECTOR (PERMANENT)
024702,003946:                                                                                                  #        NUMBER OF MARKS INCORPORATED IN MARKCTR

Page 583 

024704,003948:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF POSITION DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22 DISP METERS B-29
024705,003949:                                                                                                  #        MAGNITUDE OF VELOCITY DEVIATION (FOR DISPLAY) IN R22DISP +2 M/CSEC B-7
024706,003950:                                                                                                  #        UPDATED W-MATRIX
024707,003951: 
024708,003952:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED
024709,003953:                                                                                                  #        LM AND CSM STATE VECTORS
024710,003954:                                                                                                  #        W-MATRIX
024711,003955:                                                                                                  #        MARK TIME IN MKTIME
024712,003956:                                                                                                  #        RADAR RANGE IN RM METERS B-29
024713,003957:                                                                                                  #        RANGE RATE IN RDOTM METERS/CSEC B-7
024714,003958:                                                                                                  #        VEHUPFLG
024715,003959: 
024716,003960: 26,3200           77624        LSR22.4            CALL

024821,004065:                                                                                                  #  GETULC

024850,004094:                                                                                                  #  RADARANG
024851,004095:

024914,004158:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME LRS24.1          RR SEARCH ROUTINE
024915,004159:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO 0                      BY P VOLANTE   SDC              DATE 1-15-67
024916,004160: 
024917,004161:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION
024918,004162: 
024919,004163:                                                                                                  #  DRIVES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR IN A HEXAGONAL SEARCH PATTERN ABOUT THE LOS TO THE CSM (COMPUTED FROM THE CSM AND LM
024920,004164:                                                                                                  #  STATE VECTORS) CHECKING FOR THE DATA GOOD DISCRETE AND MONITORING THE ANGLE BETWEEN THE RADAR BORESIGHT AND THE
024921,004165:                                                                                                  #  LM +Z AXIS.  IF THIS ANGLE EXCEEDS 30 DEGREES THE PREFERRED TRACKING ATTITUDE ROUTINE IS CALLED TO PERFORM AN
024922,004166:                                                                                                  #  ATTITUDE MANEUVER.
024923,004167: 
024924,004168:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE - BANKCALL FOR LRS24.1
024925,004169:

024931,004175:                                                                                                  #        WAITLIST        FLAGUP

Page 594 

025169,004413:                                                                                                  #  PROGRAM NAME: R29     (RENDEZVOUS RADAR DESIGNATE DURING POWERED FLIGHT)
025170,004414:                                                                                                  #  MOD NO. 2     BY H. BLAIR-SMITH       JULY 2, 1968.
025171,004415: 
025172,004416:                                                                                                  #  FUNCTIONAL DESCRIPTION:
025173,004417: 
025174,004418:                                                                                                  #        DESIGNATES THE RENDEZVOUS RADAR TOWARD THE COMPUTED LOS TO THE CSM, WITH THE CHIEF OBJECTIVE OF OBTAINING RANGE
025175,004419:                                                                                                  #        AND RANGE RATE DATA AT 2-SECOND INTERVALS FOR TRANSMISSION TO THE GROUND.  WHEN THE RR IS WITHIN .5 DEGREE OF
025176,004420:                                                                                                  #        THE COMPUTED LOS, TRACKING IS ENABLED, AND DESIGNATION CONTINUES UNTIL THE DATA-GOOD DISCRETE IS RECEIVED.  AT
025177,004421:                                                                                                  #        THAT POINT, DESIGNATION CEASES AND A RADAR-READING ROUTINE TAKES OVER, PREPARING A CONSISTENT SET OF DATA FOR
025178,004422:                                                                                                  #        DOWN TELEMETRY.  THE SET INCLUDES RANGE, RANGE RATE, MARK TIME, TWO RR CDU ANGLES, THREE IMUCDU ANGLES, AND AN
025179,004423:                                                                                                  #        INDICATOR WHICH IS 1 WHEN THE SET IS CONSISTENT AND 0 OTHERWISE.  THE INDICATOR IS IN TRKMKCNT.
025180,004424: 
025181,004425:                                                                                                  #  CALLING SEQUENCE:  BEGUN EVERY 2 SECONDS AS AN INTEGRAL PART OF SERVICER
025182,004426: 
025183,004427:                                                                                                  #  SUBROUTINES CALLED:
025184,004428: 
025185,004429:                                                                                                  #        REMODE          RRTONLY
025186,004430:                                                                                                  #        UNIT            MPACVBUF
025187,004431:                                                                                                  #        QUICTRIG        AX*SR*T
025188,004432:                                                                                                  #        SPSIN           SPCOS
025189,004433:                                                                                                  #        SETRRECR        RROUT
025190,004434:                                                                                                  #        RRRDOT          RRRANGE
025191,004435: 
025192,004436:                                                                                                  #  EXIT:  TO NOR29NOW, IN SERVICER.
025193,004437: 
025194,004438:                                                                                                  #  OUTPUT:  (ALL FOR DOWNLINK)
025195,004439: 
025196,004440:                                                                                                  #        RM              RDOTM           (RAW)
025197,004441:                                                                                                  #        AIG             AMG             
025198,004442:                                                                                                  #        AOG             TRKMKCNT        TRKMKCNT = 00001 IF SET IS CONSISTENT,
025199,004443:                                                                                                  #        TANGNB          TANGNB +1       OTHERWISE TRKMKCNT = 00000.
025200,004444:                                                                                                  #        MKTIME

Page 595 

025202,004446: 
025203,004447:                                                                                                  #  ERASABLE INITIALIZATION REQUIRED:
025204,004448:

025399,004643:                                                                                                  #  R29DODES:  RR DESIGNATION LOOP FOR R29
025400,004644: 
025401,004645:                                                                                                  #  THIS ROUTINE DOES MUCH THE SAME THING AS DODES, BUT A GREAT DEAL FASTER.  IT TAKES THE NON-UNITIZED LOS VECTOR
025402,004646:                                                                                                  #  IN STABLE MEMBER COORDINATES (LOSSM) AND A DELTA-LOS IN SM AXES (LOSVDT/4) WHICH IS 1/2 SEC TIMES LOS VELOCITY,
025403,004647:                                                                                                  #  AND DEVELOPS THE SHAFT AND TRUNNION COMMANDS USING SINGLE PRECISION AS MUCH AS POSSIBLE, AND INTERPRETIVE NOT AT
025404,004648:                                                                                                  #  ALL.  THE UNIT(LOSSM + LOSVEL * 1 SEC) IS COMPUTED IN DP AND TRANSFORMED TO NAV BASE COORDINATES IN DOUBLE PRE-
025405,004649:                                                                                                  #  CISION (USING SP SINES AND COSINES OF CDU ANGLES), AND THE REST IS DONE IN SP.
025406,004650: 
025407,004651:                                                                                                  #  THE FUNCTIONAL DIFFERENCE IS THAT R29DODES ALWAYS CLEARS LOSCMFLG WHEN IT ENDS, AND IT STARTS UP THE R29READ
025408,004652:                                                                                                  #  TASK WHEN LOCK-ON IS ACHIEVED.
025409,004653: 
025410,004654: 32,2547                                           BANK     32                                    
025411,004655: 32,2000                                           SETLOC   F2DPS*32                              
025412,004656: 32,2000                                           BANK                                           
025413,004657: 
025414,004658: 32,2547                                           COUNT*   $$/R29                                
025415,004659: 32,2547  E3,1760                                  EBANK=   LOSVDT/4                              
025416,004660: 
025417,004661: 32,2547           34753        R29DODES           CA       ONE                                   
025418,004662: 32,2550           55107                           TS       TANG                                  #  INDICATE 1ST PASS THRU VECTOR LOOP.
025419,004663: 32,2551           34756                           CA       FIVE                                  
025420,004664: 
025421,004665: 32,2552           10000        R29DVBEG           CCS      A                                     #  COUNT DOWN BY TWOS IN VECTOR LOOP.
025422,004666: 32,2553           54002                           TS       Q                                     
025423,004667: 32,2554           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025424,004668: 32,2555           12563                           TCF      R29DPAS1                              #  DO THIS ON 1ST PASS THRU LOOP.
025425,004669: 
025426,004670: 32,2556           00006                           EXTEND                                         #  (A "PASS" HERE MEANS 3 TIMES AROUND).
025427,004671: 32,2557           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025428,004672: 32,2560           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025429,004673: 32,2561           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025430,004674: 32,2562           21102                           DAS      LOSSM                                 #  ADVANCE LOS VECTOR 1/2 SECOND.
025431,004675: 
025432,004676: 32,2563           00006        R29DPAS1           EXTEND                                         
025433,004677: 32,2564           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025434,004678: 32,2565           31102                           DCA      LOSSM                                 
025435,004679: 32,2566           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     #  MOVE CURRENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR LOS PRO-
025436,004680: 32,2567           52156                           DXCH     MPAC       +1                         #  JECTED 1/2 SEC AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025437,004681: 32,2570           11107                           CCS      TANG                                  
025438,004682: 32,2571           12577                           TCF      R29DVEND                              #  BUG OUT HERE IN 1ST PASS.
025439,004683: 
025440,004684: 32,2572           00006                           EXTEND                                         
025441,004685: 32,2573           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025442,004686: 32,2574           31761                           DCA      LOSVDT/4                              
025443,004687: 32,2575           50002                           INDEX    Q                                     
025444,004688: 32,2576           20156                           DAS      MPAC       +1                         #  PROJECT LOS 1 SECOND AHEAD (2ND PASS).
025445,004689: 
025446,004690: 32,2577           10002        R29DVEND           CCS      Q                                     
025447,004691: 32,2600           12552                           TCF      R29DVBEG                              #  BRANCH TO CONTINUE VECTOR LOOP.
025448,004692:

Page 601 

025450,004694:                                                                                                  #  UNITIZE AND TRANSFORM TO NAV BASE AXES THE PRESENT LOS (1ST PASS) OR THE 1-SEC PROJECTED LOS (2ND PASS).
025451,004695:
